## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[EC2NodeClass CRD] --> B[Spec Configuration]
    A --> C[Status Resolution]
    
    B --> D[AMI Selection]
    B --> E[Network Configuration]
    B --> F[Storage Configuration]
    B --> G[Instance Configuration]
    B --> H[Security Configuration]
    
    D --> D1[AMI Family]
    D --> D2[AMI Selector Terms]
    
    E --> E1[Subnet Selectors]
    E --> E2[Security Group Selectors]
    E --> E3[Public IP Association]
    
    F --> F1[Block Device Mappings]
    F --> F2[Instance Store Policy]
    
    G --> G1[Instance Profile/Role]
    G --> G2[Metadata Options]
    G --> G3[User Data]
    G --> G4[Detailed Monitoring]
    
    H --> H1[Tags]
    H --> H2[Context]
    
    C --> I[Resolved AMIs]
    C --> J[Resolved Security Groups]
    C --> K[Resolved Subnets]
    C --> L[Resolved Instance Profile]
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Defined: Create EC2NodeClass
    Defined --> Validating: Apply Configuration
    Validating --> Invalid: Validation Fails
    Validating --> Resolving: Validation Succeeds
    Invalid --> [*]: Delete Resource
    Resolving --> ResolvingAMIs: Resolve AMI Selectors
    ResolvingAMIs --> ResolvingNetworking: AMIs Found
    ResolvingAMIs --> Failed: No AMIs Found
    ResolvingNetworking --> ResolvingSubnets: Process Subnet Selectors
    ResolvingSubnets --> ResolvingSecurityGroups: Subnets Found
    ResolvingSubnets --> Failed: No Subnets Found
    ResolvingSecurityGroups --> ResolvingInstanceProfile: Security Groups Found
    ResolvingSecurityGroups --> Failed: No Security Groups Found
    ResolvingInstanceProfile --> Ready: Instance Profile Resolved
    ResolvingInstanceProfile --> Failed: Profile Resolution Failed
    Ready --> Resolving: Configuration Changed
    Ready --> [*]: Delete Resource
    Failed --> Resolving: Retry
    Failed --> [*]: Delete Resource
```
